	<script>
	$(document).ready(function(){
	$('#q1').typeahead({
		minLength: 2, // send AJAX request only after user type in at least 3 characters
	  limit: 10, // limit to show only 10 results
	  autoSelect: false,
	source: function(query, result){
		$.ajax({
			url:"search_job_title.php",
			method:"POST",
			data:{query:query},
			dataType:"json",
			success:function(data){
				result($.map(data, function(item){
					return item;
				}));
			}
		});
	}
	});

	});
	</script>

	<script>

	});
	</script>

  <script>
  function openPoslovi(evt, posloviName) {
    var i, x, tablinks;
    x = document.getElementsByClassName("poslovi");
    for (i = 0; i < x.length; i++) {
      x[i].style.display = "none";
    }
    tablinks = document.getElementsByClassName("tablink");
    for (i = 0; i < x.length; i++) {
      tablinks[i].className = tablinks[i].className.replace(" w3-red", "");
    }
    document.getElementById(posloviName).style.display = "block";
    evt.currentTarget.className += " w3-red";
  }
  </script>
